***расстраивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстраивать.html>расстра́ивать</a> (22800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстраивать.html>расстра́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstráivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disorder, to disturb, to unsettle</li>
<li>to upset, to disrupt, to derange</li>
<li>to frustrate, to derange, to thwart</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстреливать.html>расстре́ливать</a> (6869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстрелять.html>расстреля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstreljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстреливать.html>расстре́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstrélivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстрелять.html>расстреля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot, to execute (by shooting)</li>
<li>to expose to heavy (artillery or gun-) fire</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстрелять.html>расстреля́ть</a> (2576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">streljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстрелять.html>расстреля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstreljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстреливать.html>расстре́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot someone dead, to execute (by shooting)</li>
<li>to expose to heavy (artillery or gun-) fire</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́енный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstrójennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́енный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstrójennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>upset, sad, downcast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a musical instrument</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> untuned</li></ol>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находя́щийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядок.html>беспоря́дка</a>, неустройства n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Ибо в комнате его стояло нечто вроде рояля, утлая прямострунка, до того <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">расстроенная</span>, что всё исполняемое на этом, с позволения сказать, инструменте казалось подобием гамелана. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

<ol><li>огорчённый, опечаленный</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстроиться.html>расстро́иться</a> (8640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроиться.html>расстро́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstróitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстраиваться.html>расстра́иваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall into confusion</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***расстройство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a> (4622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстроить.html>расстро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstrójstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>upset, disappointment, frustration, vexation (emotions)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игру́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Proigráv igrú, ja čúvstvoval tólʹko <b>rasstrójstvo</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Having lost the game, I felt only disappointment.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Something that causes the above.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>То</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ругаться.html>руга́ется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конечно.html>коне́чно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">To što sýn mátom rugájetsja, éto konéšno <b>rasstrójstvo</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The fact that my son swears is, of course, a disappointment.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> upset, disturbance, disruption, imbalance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́ке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здуха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звать</a> сва́ливание.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rasstrójstvo</b> v potóke vózduxa nad krylóm móžet výzvatʹ sválivanije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">An upset of airflow over a wing can cause a stall.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>disorder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i>посттравмати́ческое <a href = vnd.unilang:стрессовый.html>стре́ссовое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></b></i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>posttravmatíčeskoje strɛ́ssovoje <b>rasstrójstvo</b></i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">post-traumatic stress disorder</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The state of an instrument being out of tune.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:флейта.html>фле́йты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заметно.html>заме́тно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оркестр.html>орке́стр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>на́чал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rasstrójstvo</b> mojéj fléjty stálo zamétno kak tólʹko orkéstr náčal igrátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It became apparent that my flute was out of tune as soon as the orchestra started to play.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The state of a receiver being out of tune.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">healthcare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A disease where an organ is malfunctioning.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A state of inner turmoil.</li></ol>

***расступаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расступаться.html>расступа́ться</a> (20921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расступаться.html>расступа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstupátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расступиться.html>расступи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give way, to step aside</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to open, to part</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расступиться.html>расступи́ться</a> (13472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступить.html>ступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расступиться.html>расступи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasstupítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расступаться.html>расступа́ться</a></b>)

***рассудивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́вший</a> (9042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassudívšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́ть</a> (9042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассуждать.html>рассужда́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рассу́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to argue, to reason
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассуждать.html>рассужда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rassuždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to debate, to discuss (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional case)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассуждать.html>рассужда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rassuždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to judge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rassudíte</b> nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be an arbiter between us</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рассу́живать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rassúživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***рассудок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассудок.html>рассу́док</a> (8707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудить.html>рассуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудок.html>рассу́док</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassúdok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудок.html>рассу́дка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудок.html>рассу́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассудок.html>рассу́дков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reason, sense, senses</li>
<li>judgment, mind</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитаться.html>рассчита́вшийся</a> (10896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***рассчитаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитаться.html>рассчита́ться</a> (10896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитать.html>рассчита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитаться.html>рассчита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassčitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитываться.html>рассчи́тываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle accounts <i>(with)</i>, to reckon <i>(with)</i>, to square up <i>(with)</i>, to settle up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get even, to get back some of one's own</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to number <i>(off)</i></li>
<li>to pay <i>(for)</i></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитывать.html>рассчи́тывать</a> (2088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитать.html>рассчита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитывать.html>рассчи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassčítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитать.html>рассчита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to calculate, to compute</li>
<li>to dismiss, to pay off; to sack; to discharge, to fire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to count / reckon (on); to calculate (on, upon), to depend (on, upon), to rely
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитывать.html>рассчи́тываю</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja na tebjá <b>rassčítyvaju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'<b>m counting</b> on you.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to number off, to order to number</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рассчёт</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rassčót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***рассчитываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитываться.html>рассчи́тываться</a> (21318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитывать.html>рассчи́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassčítyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитываться.html>рассчи́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rassčítyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитаться.html>рассчита́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle accounts <i>(with)</i>, to reckon <i>(with)</i>, to square up <i>(with)</i>, to settle up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get even, to get back some of one's own</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to number <i>(off)</i></li>
<li>to pay <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитываться.html>рассчи́тываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проступок.html>просту́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rassčítyvatʹsja</b> za svoí prostúpki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay for one's actions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассчитывать.html>рассчи́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rassčítyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
